The implementation spans both server-side coordinators and client-side membership managers.\\n\\n**Classic Group State Machine (org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.classic):**\\n\\nThe ClassicGroupState enum (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroupState.java) defines five states with specific valid transitions:\\n\\n- EMPTY: Initial state where the group has no members. Transitions to PREPARING_REBALANCE when members join.\\n- PREPARING_REBALANCE (Join Phase): Group waits for members to join within a timeout period. Members send JoinGroup requests. Transitions to COMPLETING_REBALANCE when a leader is elected or timeout occurs.\\n- COMPLETING_REBALANCE (Sync Phase): Group waits for leader to compute assignments and members to send SyncGroup requests. Transitions to STABLE when all members have synced.\\n- STABLE: Active rebalance state where members can fetch and consume with current assignments. Transitions back to PREPARING_REBALANCE if a member fails, leaves, or updates metadata.\\n- DEAD: Final state before cleanup. Can transition from any other state.\\n\\nThe ClassicGroup class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java) manages the group state and enforces valid transitions. ClassicGroupMember (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroupMember.java) tracks individual member state with awaitingJoinFuture and awaitingSyncFuture for coordination.\\n\\n**Modern Consumer Group State Machine (org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.modern.consumer):**\\n\\nThe ConsumerGroup class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java) implements an updated state machine with states:\\n\\n- EMPTY: No members in the group.\\n- ASSIGNING: Group is computing target assignments for all members using partition assignors.\\n- RECONCILING: Members are reconciling to their target assignments (pulling assignments and revoking previous partitions).\\n- STABLE: All members have completed reconciliation and are in steady state.\\n- DEAD: Group is marked for deletion.\\n\\nThe transitions flow as: EMPTY → ASSIGNING → RECONCILING → STABLE, with the ability to return to ASSIGNING from STABLE when metadata changes trigger rebalancing. ConsumerGroupMember (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroupMember.java) manages member-specific state.\\n\\n**Share Group State Machine (org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.modern.share):**\\n\\nThe ShareGroup class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/share/ShareGroup.java) implements a simpler state machine:\\n\\n- EMPTY: No members.\\n- STABLE: Members are actively consuming.\\n- DEAD: Group being removed.\\n- UNKNOWN: Initial/fallback state.\\n\\n**Streams Group State Machine (org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.streams):**\\n\\nThe StreamsGroup class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/streams/StreamsGroup.java) implements:\\n\\n- EMPTY: No members.\\n- NOT_READY: Group cannot assign tasks (topology not ready).\\n- ASSIGNING: Computing task assignments.\\n- RECONCILING: Members reconciling task assignments.\\n- STABLE: All members have tasks assigned and reconciled.\\n- DEAD: Group being removed.\\n\\n**State Transition Orchestration:**\\n\\nThe GroupMetadataManager class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManager.java) is the central coordinator managing all state transitions. It handles JoinGroup requests (initiating rebalance), SyncGroup requests (completing rebalance), heartbeats (maintaining stable state), and member departures (triggering new rebalance).\\n\\n**Client-Side State Enums:**\\n\\nClient-side representations are provided in:\\n- clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/ClassicGroupState.java\\n- clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/ConsumerGroupState.java (deprecated)\\n- clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/GroupState.java (unified enum)\\n\\n**Member State Management:**\\n\\nThe MemberState enum (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/MemberState.java) tracks individual member reconciliation states separate from group-level states, enabling fine-grained tracking of member progress through assignment reconciliation (UNJOINED → JOINING → STABLE → RECONCILING → ACKNOWLEDGING → LEAVING → UNSUBSCRIBED).\\n\\nThe state machines implement the Kafka rebalancing protocol with Join (PREPARING_REBALANCE in classic, ASSIGNING in modern), Sync (COMPLETING_REBALANCE in classic, RECONCILING in modern), and Stable (STABLE across all types) phases, ensuring coordinated group membership changes and assignment distribution.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":779,"cache_read_input_tokens":98659,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":779},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"ee3b3d01-c93f-4887-a448-7c05851be4d4","uuid":"cda59dc7-77e1-448e-8fec-1394b6bf8a25"}

It handles JoinGroup requests (initiating rebalance), SyncGroup requests (completing rebalance), heartbeats (maintaining stable state), and member departures (triggering new rebalance).\\n\\n**Client-Side State Enums:**\\n\\nClient-side representations are provided in:\\n- clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/ClassicGroupState.java\\n- clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/ConsumerGroupState.java (deprecated)\\n- clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/GroupState.java (unified enum)\\n\\n**Member State Management:**\\n\\nThe MemberState enum (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/MemberState.java) tracks individual member reconciliation states separate from group-level states, enabling fine-grained tracking of member progress through assignment reconciliation (UNJOINED → JOINING → STABLE → RECONCILING → ACKNOWLEDGING → LEAVING → UNSUBSCRIBED).\\n\\nThe state machines implement the Kafka rebalancing protocol with Join (PREPARING_REBALANCE in classic, ASSIGNING in modern), Sync (COMPLETING_REBALANCE in classic, RECONCILING in modern), and Stable (STABLE across all types) phases, ensuring coordinated group membership changes and assignment distribution.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

The implementation spans both server-side coordinators and client-side membership managers.\\n\\n**Classic Group State Machine (org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.classic):**\\n\\nThe ClassicGroupState enum (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroupState.java) defines five states with specific valid transitions:\\n\\n- EMPTY: Initial state where the group has no members. Transitions to PREPARING_REBALANCE when members join.\\n- PREPARING_REBALANCE (Join Phase): Group waits for members to join within a timeout period. Members send JoinGroup requests. Transitions to COMPLETING_REBALANCE when a leader is elected or timeout occurs.\\n- COMPLETING_REBALANCE (Sync Phase): Group waits for leader to compute assignments and members to send SyncGroup requests. Transitions to STABLE when all members have synced.\\n- STABLE: Active rebalance state where members can fetch and consume with current assignments. Transitions back to PREPARING_REBALANCE if a member fails, leaves, or updates metadata.\\n- DEAD: Final state before cleanup. Can transition from any other state.\\n\\nThe ClassicGroup class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java) manages the group state and enforces valid transitions. ClassicGroupMember (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroupMember.java) tracks individual member state with awaitingJoinFuture and awaitingSyncFuture for coordination.\\n\\n**Modern Consumer Group State Machine (org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.modern.consumer):**\\n\\nThe ConsumerGroup class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java) implements an updated state machine with states:\\n\\n- EMPTY: No members in the group.\\n- ASSIGNING: Group is computing target assignments for all members using partition assignors.\\n- RECONCILING: Members are reconciling to their target assignments (pulling assignments and revoking previous partitions).\\n- STABLE: All members have completed reconciliation and are in steady state.\\n- DEAD: Group is marked for deletion.\\n\\nThe transitions flow as: EMPTY → ASSIGNING → RECONCILING → STABLE, with the ability to return to ASSIGNING from STABLE when metadata changes trigger rebalancing. ConsumerGroupMember (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroupMember.java) manages member-specific state.\\n\\n**Share Group State Machine (org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.modern.share):**\\n\\nThe ShareGroup class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/share/ShareGroup.java) implements a simpler state machine:\\n\\n- EMPTY: No members.\\n- STABLE: Members are actively consuming.\\n- DEAD: Group being removed.\\n- UNKNOWN: Initial/fallback state.\\n\\n**Streams Group State Machine (org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.streams):**\\n\\nThe StreamsGroup class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/streams/StreamsGroup.java) implements:\\n\\n- EMPTY: No members.\\n- NOT_READY: Group cannot assign tasks (topology not ready).\\n- ASSIGNING: Computing task assignments.\\n- RECONCILING: Members reconciling task assignments.\\n- STABLE: All members have tasks assigned and reconciled.\\n- DEAD: Group being removed.\\n\\n**State Transition Orchestration:**\\n\\nThe GroupMetadataManager class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManager.java) is the central coordinator managing all state transitions. \"GroupState\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Kafka consumer group coordinator implements multiple state machines for managing different group types and member participation. The implementation spans both server-side coordinators and client-side membership managers.\\n\\n**Classic Group State Machine (org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.classic):**\\n\\nThe ClassicGroupState enum (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroupState.java) defines five states with specific valid transitions:\\n\\n- EMPTY: Initial state where the group has no members. Transitions to PREPARING_REBALANCE when members join.\\n- PREPARING_REBALANCE (Join Phase): Group waits for members to join within a timeout period. Members send JoinGroup requests. Transitions to COMPLETING_REBALANCE when a leader is elected or timeout occurs.\\n- COMPLETING_REBALANCE (Sync Phase): Group waits for leader to compute assignments and members to send SyncGroup requests. Transitions to STABLE when all members have synced.\\n- STABLE: Active rebalance state where members can fetch and consume with current assignments. Transitions back to PREPARING_REBALANCE if a member fails, leaves, or updates metadata.\\n- DEAD: Final state before cleanup. Can transition from any other state.\\n\\nThe ClassicGroup class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java) manages the group state and enforces valid transitions. ClassicGroupMember (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroupMember.java) tracks individual member state with awaitingJoinFuture and awaitingSyncFuture for coordination.\\n\\n**Modern Consumer Group State Machine (org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.modern.consumer):**\\n\\nThe ConsumerGroup class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java) implements an updated state machine with states:\\n\\n- EMPTY: No members in the group.\\n- ASSIGNING: Group is computing target assignments for all members using partition assignors.\\n- RECONCILING: Members are reconciling to their target assignments (pulling assignments and revoking previous partitions).\\n- STABLE: All members have completed reconciliation and are in steady state.\\n- DEAD: Group is marked for deletion.\\n\\nThe transitions flow as: EMPTY → ASSIGNING → RECONCILING → STABLE, with the ability to return to ASSIGNING from STABLE when metadata changes trigger rebalancing. ConsumerGroupMember (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroupMember.java) manages member-specific state.\\n\\n**Share Group State Machine (org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.modern.share):**\\n\\nThe ShareGroup class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/share/ShareGroup.java) implements a simpler state machine:\\n\\n- EMPTY: No members.\\n- STABLE: Members are actively consuming.\\n- DEAD: Group being removed.\\n- UNKNOWN: Initial/fallback state.\\n\\n**Streams Group State Machine (org.apache.kafka.coordinator.group.streams):**\\n\\nThe StreamsGroup class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/streams/StreamsGroup.java) implements:\\n\\n- EMPTY: No members.\\n- NOT_READY: Group cannot assign tasks (topology not ready).\\n- ASSIGNING: Computing task assignments.\\n- RECONCILING: Members reconciling task assignments.\\n- STABLE: All members have tasks assigned and reconciled.\\n- DEAD: Group being removed.\\n\\n**State Transition Orchestration:**\\n\\nThe GroupMetadataManager class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManager.java) is the central coordinator managing all state transitions. It handles JoinGroup requests (initiating rebalance), SyncGroup requests (completing rebalance), heartbeats (maintaining stable state), and member departures (triggering new rebalance).\\n\\n**Client-Side State Enums:**\\n\\nClient-side representations are provided in:\\n- clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/ClassicGroupState.java\\n- clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/ConsumerGroupState.java (deprecated)\\n- clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/GroupState.java (unified enum)\\n\\n**Member State Management:**\\n\\nThe MemberState enum (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/MemberState.java) tracks individual member reconciliation states separate from group-level states, enabling fine-grained tracking of member progress through assignment reconciliation (UNJOINED → JOINING → STABLE → RECONCILING → ACKNOWLEDGING → LEAVING → UNSUBSCRIBED).\\n\\nThe state machines implement the Kafka rebalancing protocol with Join (PREPARING_REBALANCE in classic, ASSIGNING in modern), Sync (COMPLETING_REBALANCE in classic, RECONCILING in modern), and Stable (STABLE across all types) phases, ensuring coordinated group membership changes and assignment distribution.\"\n}\n","numLines":156,"startLine":1,"totalLines":156}}}
